| expressive | 표정(표현력)이 풍부한 | His face was very expressive. |

| have difficulty -ing | ~하는 데 고생하다 | I have difficulty understanding this. |
| healthful | 건강에 좋은 | Eating vegetables is healthful. |
| hillside | 비탈, 산비탈 | Flowers grew on the green hillside. |
| junction | 교차로, 나들목 | The accident happened at the road junction. |
| justification | 정당화, 합리화, 타당한 이유 | He gave no justification for his actions. |
| lodge | 숙박시키다, 투숙시키다 | They will lodge you in a hotel. |
| lodge | 숙박시키다, 투숙시키다 | They will lodge you in a hotel. |
| mandate | 명령하다, 요구하다, 권한을 주다 | The court will mandate a new trial. |
| mandate | 명령하다, 요구하다, 권한을 주다 | The court will mandate a new trial. |
| marketing | (상품 판매를 위한) 홍보, 마케팅 | Good marketing increases product sales. |
| mortal | 치명적인 | The poison was mortal. |
| mortal | 치명적인 | The poison was mortal. |
| reflect on ~ | ~에 대해 반성하다, 곰곰이 생각하다 | I reflect on my past mistakes. |
| stoop | 몸을 굽히다, 구부리다 | He had to stoop to enter the small door. |
| strap | 끈으로 묶다 | They will strap the luggage to the roof. |
| strap | 끈으로 묶다 | They will strap the luggage to the roof. |
| swan | 백조 | A beautiful swan glided on the lake. |
| take ~ apart | ~을 분해하다 | I will take the engine apart. |
| thrust | 찌르기 | The spear will thrust forward. |
| thrust | 찌르기 | The spear will thrust forward. |
| timely | 시기적절한, 적시의 | Your help was very timely. |
| treaty | 조약, 협정 | The two countries signed a peace treaty. |
